# extract_images_from_excel.py
import openpyxl
from openpyxl.drawing.image import Image
import os
from PIL import Image as PILImage
import requests
from io import BytesIO

class ExcelImageExtractor:
    def __init__(self, excel_file):
        self.excel_file = excel_file
        self.images = []
        
    def extract_images(self):
        """Tr√≠ch xu·∫•t h√¨nh ·∫£nh t·ª´ Excel"""
        wb = openpyxl.load_workbook(self.excel_file)
        
        for sheet in wb.worksheets:
            print(f"ƒêang x·ª≠ l√Ω sheet: {sheet.title}")
            
            # L·∫•y t·∫•t c·∫£ h√¨nh ·∫£nh trong sheet
            if sheet._images:
                for idx, img in enumerate(sheet._images):
                    # L∆∞u h√¨nh ·∫£nh
                    img_data = img._data()
                    filename = f"extracted_image_{sheet.title}_{idx+1}.png"
                    
                    with open(filename, 'wb') as f:
                        f.write(img_data)
                    print(f"  ‚úÖ ƒê√£ l∆∞u: {filename}")
                    self.images.append(filename)
            
            # ƒê·ªçc d·ªØ li·ªáu t·ª´ cells
            for row in sheet.iter_rows(min_row=1, max_row=10):
                for cell in row:
                    if cell.value and ('http' in str(cell.value).lower()):
                        print(f"  üîó T√¨m th·∫•y link: {cell.value}")
        
        print(f"\n‚úÖ T·ªïng c·ªông: {len(self.images)} h√¨nh ·∫£nh")
        return self.images
    
    def create_post_with_images(self):
        """T·∫°o b√†i vi·∫øt k√®m h√¨nh ·∫£nh"""
        posts = []
        
        for idx, img_path in enumerate(self.images):
            # T·∫°o n·ªôi dung b√†i vi·∫øt
            content = f"""
========================================
B√ÄI VI·∫æT AFFILIATE {idx+1} K√àM H√åNH ·∫¢NH
========================================

üî• SHOPEE 6.6 MEGA SALE üî•

[H√åNH ·∫¢NH: {img_path}]

‚ú® ∆ØU ƒê√ÉI ƒê·∫∂C BI·ªÜT:
‚Ä¢ Gi·∫£m gi√° ƒë·∫øn 50%
‚Ä¢ Freeship 0ƒê to√†n qu·ªëc
‚Ä¢ Voucher Xtra 6 tri·ªáu ƒë·ªìng

üõçÔ∏è MUA NGAY: https://shorten.asia/cBGVb2kE

#Shopee6_6 #Sale #Affiliate
"""
            post_file = f"post_with_image_{idx+1}.txt"
            with open(post_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write(content)
            posts.append(post_file)
            print(f"‚úÖ ƒê√£ t·∫°o: {post_file}")
        
        return posts

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Ch·ªâ ƒë·ªãnh file Excel c·ªßa b·∫°n
    excel_file = "your_file.xlsx"  # ƒê·ªïi t√™n file c·ªßa b·∫°n
    
    if os.path.exists(excel_file):
        extractor = ExcelImageExtractor(excel_file)
        images = extractor.extract_images()
        posts = extractor.create_post_with_images()
        print(f"\n‚úÖ Ho√†n th√†nh! {len(images)} ·∫£nh, {len(posts)} b√†i vi·∫øt")
    else:
        print(f"‚ùå Kh√¥ng t√¨m th·∫•y file: {excel_file}")
        print("Vui l√≤ng ƒë·∫£m b·∫£o file Excel ·ªü c√πng th∆∞ m·ª•c")

--- FILE: facebook_complete.py ---

import time
import json
from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys

class CompleteFacebookAgent:
    """X? l˝ t?t c? c·c lo?i popup c?a Facebook"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.driver = None
    
    def handle_all_popups(self):
        """X? l˝ t?t c? popup cÛ th? xu?t hi?n"""
        
        popup_handlers = [
            # Popup thÙng b·o trÏnh duy?t
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Cho phÈp')]", "Cho phÈp"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Allow')]", "Allow"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), '–?ng ˝')]", "–?ng ˝"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'OK')]", "OK"),
            
            # Popup luu m?t kh?u
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'KhÙng')]", "KhÙng"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Not Now')]", "Not Now"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'B? qua')]", "B? qua"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Skip')]", "Skip"),
            
            # Popup dÛng
            ("//div[@aria-label='–Ûng']", "–Ûng"),
            ("//div[@aria-label='Close']", "Close"),
            ("//div[@role='button'][contains(., '◊')]", "◊"),
            
            # Popup thÙng b·o
            ("//div[@aria-label='B? qua']", "B? qua"),
            ("//div[@aria-label='Dismiss']", "Dismiss"),
        ]
        
        closed_count = 0
        for selector, name in popup_handlers:
            try:
                elements = self.driver.find_elements(By.XPATH, selector)
                for elem in elements:
                    if elem.is_displayed():
                        try:
                            elem.click()
                            closed_count += 1
                            print(f"   ? –„ x? l˝ popup: {name}")
                            time.sleep(1)
                        except:
                            pass
            except:
                continue
        
        # C·ch 2: Nh?n ESC d? dÛng popup
        if closed_count == 0:
            try:
                from selenium.webdriver.common.action_chains import ActionChains
                actions = ActionChains(self.driver)
                actions.send_keys(Keys.ESCAPE).perform()
                print("   ? –„ nh?n ESC d? dÛng popup")
                time.sleep(1)
            except:
                pass
        
        return closed_count
    
    def wait_for_page_ready(self, max_wait=10):
        """Ch? trang t?i xong v‡ popup xu?t hi?n"""
        for i in range(max_wait):
            time.sleep(1)
            # Ki?m tra n?u cÛ popup thÏ x? l˝
            if self.handle_all_popups() > 0:
                print(f"   –„ x? l˝ popup ? gi‚y th? {i+1}")
    
    def login(self):
        """–ang nh?p b?ng cookie"""
        print("?? Kh?i d?ng trÏnh duy?t...")
        
        options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
        options.add_argument('--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled')
        options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
        options.add_argument('--disable-infobars')
        options.add_argument('--lang=vi-VN')
        options.add_experimental_option('excludeSwitches', ['enable-automation'])
        
        self.driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options)
        self.driver.execute_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        self.driver.get("https://www.facebook.com/")
        print("? –?i trang t?i...")
        time.sleep(3)
        
        # X? l˝ popup ngay sau khi v‡o trang
        self.handle_all_popups()
        
        # Load cookie
        try:
            with open("fb_cookies_selenium.json", "r") as f:
                cookies = json.load(f)
            for cookie in cookies:
                try:
                    self.driver.add_cookie(cookie)
                except:
                    pass
            
            self.driver.refresh()
            print("? –?i cookie du?c ·p d?ng...")
            time.sleep(4)
            
            # X? l˝ popup sau refresh
            self.handle_all_popups()
            self.wait_for_page_ready()
            
            print("? –„ dang nh?p th‡nh cÙng!")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"?? L?i: {e}")
            return False
    
    def post(self, content):
        """–ang b‡i lÍn Facebook"""
        
        print("\n?? B?t d?u dang b‡i...")
        
        # X? l˝ popup tru?c khi tÏm Ù dang b‡i
        self.handle_all_popups()
        
        # C·ch 1: D˘ng phÌm t?t 'c' (nhanh nh?t)
        try:
            from selenium.webdriver.common.action_chains import ActionChains
            actions = ActionChains(self.driver)
            actions.send_keys('c').perform()
            print("   ?? D˘ng phÌm t?t 'c' d? m? khung dang b‡i")
            time.sleep(2)
        except:
            pass
        
        # C·ch 2: TÏm v‡ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i
        post_selectors = [
            "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'T?o b‡i vi?t')]",
            "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'Create a post')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), 'B?n dang nghi gÏ')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), \"What's on your mind\")]"
        ]
        
        for selector in post_selectors:
            try:
                elem = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if elem.is_displayed():
                    self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", elem)
                    print("   ? –„ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i")
                    time.sleep(2)
                    break
            except:
                continue
        
        # TÏm khung nh?p n?i dung
        editor = None
        editor_selectors = [
            "//div[@role='textbox']",
            "//div[@contenteditable='true']",
            "//div[@aria-label='What\'s on your mind?']",
            "//div[@aria-label='B?n dang nghi gÏ?']"
        ]
        
        for selector in editor_selectors:
            try:
                editor = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if editor.is_displayed():
                    break
            except:
                continue
        
        if editor:
            try:
                editor.click()
            except:
                self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", editor)
            
            editor.send_keys(content)
            print("   ? –„ nh?p n?i dung")
            time.sleep(1)
        else:
            print("   ? KhÙng tÏm th?y khung nh?p")
            return False
        
        # TÏm n˙t dang
        btn_selectors = [
            "//div[@aria-label='–ang']",
            "//div[@aria-label='Post']",
            "//div[contains(text(), '–ang')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), 'Post')]"
        ]
        
        for selector in btn_selectors:
            try:
                btn = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if btn.is_displayed():
                    self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", btn)
                    print("   ? –„ click n˙t –ang")
                    time.sleep(3)
                    print("\n?? –ANG B¿I TH¿NH C‘NG!")
                    return True
            except:
                continue
        
        # Th? Ctrl+Enter
        try:
            editor.send_keys(Keys.CONTROL, Keys.ENTER)
            print("   ? –„ d˘ng Ctrl+Enter")
            time.sleep(3)
            print("\n?? –ANG B¿I TH¿NH C‘NG!")
            return True
        except:
            print("   ? KhÙng th? dang b‡i")
            return False
    
    def close(self):
        if self.driver:
            self.driver.quit()
            print("?? –„ dÛng trÏnh duy?t")

def main():
    print("=" * 50)
    print("?? FACEBOOK POSTER - COMPLETE AGENT")
    print("   (X? l˝ m?i lo?i popup)")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    content = """Xin ch‡o b?n, hÙm nay ch˙ng ta s? c˘ng nhau di qua m?t h‡nh trÏnh nh? mang tÍn "BuÙng b?". 

CÛ nh?ng di?u trong cu?c s?ng khi?n ta n?ng lÚng, nhung dÙi khi, vi?c gi? ch?t l?i ch? l‡m ta thÍm m?t m?i. 

H„y th? hÌt m?t hoi th?t s‚uÖ v‡ th? ra th?t ch?mÖ d? c?m nh?n s? nh? nhım. 

B?n x?ng d·ng du?c bÏnh an, ngay trong kho?nh kh?c n‡y.

#BuongBo #BinhAn #TamLy

thÌ nghi?m 12 - Complete Agent

Th‡nh cÙng!"""
    
    agent = CompleteFacebookAgent()
    
    if agent.login():
        agent.post(content)
    else:
        print("? KhÙng th? dang nh?p")
        print("?? H„y ch?y: python save_cookie_manual.py")
    
    input("\n?? Nh?n Enter d? dÛng trÏnh duy?t...")
    agent.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

--- FILE: facebook_poster.py ---

"""
Facebook Auto Poster - Ch?y riÍng, cÛ x? l˝ l?i token
"""
import requests
import time
import json
import os
from datetime import datetime
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

class FacebookPoster:
    def __init__(self):
        self.page_id = os.getenv("FACEBOOK_PAGE_ID")
        self.access_token = os.getenv("FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN")
        self.posts_file = "safe_post.txt"
    
    def check_token(self):
        """Ki?m tra token cÛ h?p l? khÙng"""
        if not self.access_token or 'your_' in self.access_token:
            print("? Token chua du?c c?u hÏnh!")
            return False
        
        url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{self.page_id}?access_token={self.access_token}"
        try:
            response = requests.get(url, timeout=10)
            if response.status_code == 200:
                print(f"? Token h?p l?! Page: {response.json().get('name')}")
                return True
            else:
                print(f"? Token khÙng h?p l?: {response.status_code}")
                return False
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"? L?i k?t n?i: {e}")
            return False
    
    def post_to_facebook(self, message):
        """–ang b‡i lÍn Facebook"""
        url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/{self.page_id}/feed"
        data = {
            "message": message,
            "access_token": self.access_token
        }
        
        try:
            response = requests.post(url, data=data, timeout=30)
            if response.status_code == 200:
                result = response.json()
                print(f"? –„ dang b‡i: {message[:50]}...")
                print(f"   Post ID: {result.get('id')}")
                return True
            else:
                error = response.json()
                print(f"? L?i {response.status_code}: {error.get('error', {}).get('message', 'Unknown')}")
                return False
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"? L?i: {e}")
            return False
    
    def load_post_content(self):
        """T?i n?i dung b‡i dang t? file"""
        try:
            with open(self.posts_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read().strip()
            if content:
                return content
        except:
            pass
        
        # N?i dung m?c d?nh
        return """?? UU –√I H?P D?N T? SHOPEE

? Gi?m gi· d?n 70%
? Freeship to‡n qu?c
? Voucher d?n 5 tri?u

?? Xem chi ti?t: https://go.isclix.com/deep_link/v6/6983938396644077046/4751584435713464237?sub4=sen_v3

#MuaSam #SaleOff #GiamGia"""
    
    def run_once(self):
        """Ch?y dang b‡i 1 l?n"""
        print("=" * 60)
        print("?? FACEBOOK AUTO POSTER")
        print("=" * 60)
        
        if not self.check_token():
            print("?? Vui lÚng c?p nh?t FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN trong .env")
            print("   Hu?ng d?n: https://developers.facebook.com/tools/explorer/")
            return
        
        content = self.load_post_content()
        print(f"\n?? N?i dung s? dang:\n{content}\n")
        
        result = self.post_to_facebook(content)
        if result:
            print("\n? –ang b‡i th‡nh cÙng!")
        else:
            print("\n? –ang b‡i th?t b?i. Ki?m tra token v‡ quy?n.")
    
    def run_loop(self, interval_minutes=60):
        """Ch?y l?p l?i m?i interval ph˙t"""
        print(f"?? S? dang b‡i m?i {interval_minutes} ph˙t")
        
        while True:
            self.run_once()
            print(f"\n? Ch? {interval_minutes} ph˙t d?n l?n dang ti?p theo...")
            time.sleep(interval_minutes * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    poster = FacebookPoster()
    
    # Ch?y 1 l?n
    poster.run_once()
    
    # Ho?c ch?y l?p l?i (b? comment dÚng du?i)
    # poster.run_loop(interval_minutes=60)

--- FILE: facebook_poster_fixed.py ---

import time
import json
from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys

class FixedFacebookAgent:
    """PhiÍn b?n x? l˝ popup v‡ overlay"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.driver = None
    
    def close_popups(self):
        """–Ûng c·c popup cÛ th? xu?t hi?n"""
        
        popup_selectors = [
            "//div[@aria-label='–Ûng']",
            "//div[@aria-label='Close']",
            "//div[contains(@class, 'x1i10hfl')][contains(text(), '–Ûng')]",
            "//div[@role='button'][contains(., 'B? qua')]",
            "//div[@role='button'][contains(., 'Skip')]",
            "//div[@role='button'][contains(., 'Not Now')]",
            "//div[@role='button'][contains(., 'KhÙng ph?i b‚y gi?')]"
        ]
        
        for selector in popup_selectors:
            try:
                popup = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if popup.is_displayed():
                    popup.click()
                    print("   ? –„ dÛng popup")
                    time.sleep(1)
            except:
                continue
    
    def click_by_js(self, element):
        """Click b?ng JavaScript (vu?t qua m?i overlay)"""
        self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", element)
        return True
    
    def find_and_click_post_box(self):
        """TÏm v‡ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i b?ng nhi?u c·ch"""
        
        selectors = [
            "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'T?o b‡i vi?t')]",
            "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'Create a post')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), 'B?n dang nghi gÏ')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), \"What's on your mind\")]",
            "//div[@role='button'][contains(@class, 'x1i10hfl')]//span[contains(text(), 'B?n dang nghi gÏ')]"
        ]
        
        for selector in selectors:
            try:
                elem = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if elem.is_displayed():
                    # Th? click thu?ng
                    try:
                        elem.click()
                    except:
                        # N?u b? ch?n, d˘ng JavaScript
                        self.click_by_js(elem)
                    print(f"   ? –„ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i")
                    return True
            except:
                continue
        
        # C·ch cu?i: D˘ng phÌm t?t 'c' d? m? h?p tho?i
        try:
            from selenium.webdriver.common.action_chains import ActionChains
            actions = ActionChains(self.driver)
            actions.send_keys('c').perform()
            print("   ? –„ d˘ng phÌm t?t 'c' d? m? h?p tho?i")
            return True
        except:
            pass
        
        return False
    
    def login(self):
        """–ang nh?p b?ng cookie"""
        options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
        options.add_argument('--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled')
        options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
        options.add_argument('--disable-infobars')
        options.add_argument('--lang=vi-VN')
        
        self.driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options)
        self.driver.execute_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        self.driver.get("https://www.facebook.com/")
        time.sleep(3)
        
        # –Ûng popup n?u cÛ
        self.close_popups()
        
        try:
            with open("fb_cookies_selenium.json", "r") as f:
                cookies = json.load(f)
            for cookie in cookies:
                try:
                    self.driver.add_cookie(cookie)
                except:
                    pass
            self.driver.refresh()
            time.sleep(4)
            print("? –„ dang nh?p b?ng cookie")
            
            # –Ûng popup sau khi refresh
            self.close_popups()
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"?? KhÙng load du?c cookie: {e}")
            return False
    
    def post(self, content):
        """–ang b‡i lÍn Facebook"""
        
        print("\n?? B?t d?u dang b‡i...")
        
        # –Ûng popup tru?c khi tÏm Ù dang b‡i
        self.close_popups()
        
        # TÏm v‡ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i
        if not self.find_and_click_post_box():
            print("? KhÙng tÏm th?y Ù dang b‡i")
            return False
        
        time.sleep(2)
        
        # TÏm khung nh?p n?i dung
        editor_selectors = [
            "//div[@role='textbox']",
            "//div[@contenteditable='true']",
            "//div[@aria-label='What\'s on your mind?']",
            "//div[@aria-label='B?n dang nghi gÏ?']"
        ]
        
        editor = None
        for selector in editor_selectors:
            try:
                editor = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if editor.is_displayed():
                    break
            except:
                continue
        
        if editor:
            try:
                editor.click()
            except:
                self.click_by_js(editor)
            editor.send_keys(content)
            time.sleep(1)
            print("? –„ nh?p n?i dung")
        else:
            print("? KhÙng tÏm th?y khung nh?p")
            return False
        
        # TÏm n˙t dang
        btn_selectors = [
            "//div[@aria-label='–ang']",
            "//div[@aria-label='Post']",
            "//div[contains(text(), '–ang')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), 'Post')]"
        ]
        
        for selector in btn_selectors:
            try:
                post_btn = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if post_btn.is_displayed():
                    try:
                        post_btn.click()
                    except:
                        self.click_by_js(post_btn)
                    time.sleep(3)
                    print("?? –ANG B¿I TH¿NH C‘NG!")
                    return True
            except:
                continue
        
        # Th? d˘ng phÌm t?t Ctrl+Enter
        try:
            editor.send_keys(Keys.CONTROL, Keys.ENTER)
            time.sleep(3)
            print("? –„ d˘ng Ctrl+Enter d? dang b‡i")
            return True
        except:
            print("? KhÙng tÏm th?y n˙t dang")
            return False
    
    def close(self):
        if self.driver:
            self.driver.quit()
            print("?? –„ dÛng trÏnh duy?t")

def main():
    print("=" * 50)
    print("?? FACEBOOK POSTER - FIXED AGENT")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    content = """Xin ch‡o b?n, hÙm nay ch˙ng ta s? c˘ng nhau di qua m?t h‡nh trÏnh nh? mang tÍn "BuÙng b?". 

CÛ nh?ng di?u trong cu?c s?ng khi?n ta n?ng lÚng, nhung dÙi khi, vi?c gi? ch?t l?i ch? l‡m ta thÍm m?t m?i. 

H„y th? hÌt m?t hoi th?t s‚uÖ v‡ th? ra th?t ch?mÖ d? c?m nh?n s? nh? nhım. 

B?n x?ng d·ng du?c bÏnh an, ngay trong kho?nh kh?c n‡y.

#BuongBo #BinhAn #TamLy

thÌ nghi?m 11 - Fixed Agent

Th‡nh cÙng!"""
    
    agent = FixedFacebookAgent()
    
    if agent.login():
        agent.post(content)
    else:
        print("? KhÙng th? dang nh?p")
    
    input("\n?? Nh?n Enter d? dÛng trÏnh duy?t...")
    agent.close()

    main()

--- FILE: facebook_stepbystep.py ---

import time
import json
from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys

class StepByStepFacebookAgent:
    """Ch?y t?ng bu?c, ch? x·c nh?n c?a ngu?i d˘ng"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.driver = None
    
    def wait_for_user(self, step_name, instruction):
        """Ch? ngu?i d˘ng x·c nh?n tru?c khi ti?p t?c"""
        print("\n" + "=" * 60)
        print(f"?? BU?C: {step_name}")
        print(f"?? HU?NG D?N: {instruction}")
        print("=" * 60)
        response = input("?? –„ s?n s‡ng? (y/n/yes d? ti?p t?c, ho?c nh?n Enter d? ti?p): ")
        return response.lower() in ['y', 'yes', '']
    
    def login(self):
        """–ang nh?p b?ng cookie - t?ng bu?c"""
        
        if not self.wait_for_user("M? TRÃNH DUY?T", "Script s? m? Chrome v‡ v‡o Facebook"):
            return False
        
        print("?? –ang kh?i d?ng Chrome...")
        options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
        options.add_argument('--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled')
        options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
        options.add_argument('--disable-infobars')
        options.add_argument('--lang=vi-VN')
        
        self.driver = webdriver.Chrome(options=options)
        self.driver.execute_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")
        
        self.driver.get("https://www.facebook.com/")
        print("? –„ m? Facebook")
        time.sleep(3)
        
        if not self.wait_for_user("T?I COOKIE", "Script s? load cookie d? dang nh?p t? d?ng"):
            return False
        
        try:
            with open("fb_cookies_selenium.json", "r") as f:
                cookies = json.load(f)
            for cookie in cookies:
                try:
                    self.driver.add_cookie(cookie)
                except:
                    pass
            self.driver.refresh()
            print("? –„ load cookie v‡ refresh trang")
            time.sleep(4)
            
            if not self.wait_for_user("KI?M TRA –ANG NH?P", "H„y nhÏn trÏnh duy?t xem d„ dang nh?p th‡nh cÙng chua?"):
                return False
            
            print("? –ang nh?p th‡nh cÙng!")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"? L?i: {e}")
            return False
    
    def handle_popups(self):
        """X? l˝ popup - t?ng bu?c"""
        
        if not self.wait_for_user("X? L› POPUP", "Script s? tÏm v‡ dÛng c·c popup (thÙng b·o, cho phÈp...)"):
            return
        
        popup_selectors = [
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Cho phÈp')]", "Cho phÈp"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Allow')]", "Allow"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'KhÙng')]", "KhÙng"),
            ("//button[contains(text(), 'Not Now')]", "Not Now"),
            ("//div[@aria-label='–Ûng']", "–Ûng"),
        ]
        
        closed = 0
        for selector, name in popup_selectors:
            try:
                elements = self.driver.find_elements(By.XPATH, selector)
                for elem in elements:
                    if elem.is_displayed():
                        elem.click()
                        closed += 1
                        print(f"   ? –„ dÛng popup: {name}")
                        time.sleep(1)
            except:
                continue
        
        if closed == 0:
            print("   ?? KhÙng th?y popup n‡o")
        
        self.wait_for_user("X¡C NH?N POPUP", "H„y nhÏn trÏnh duy?t, popup d„ du?c x? l˝ chua?")
    
    def find_post_box(self):
        """TÏm Ù dang b‡i - t?ng bu?c"""
        
        if not self.wait_for_user("TÃM ‘ –ANG B¿I", "Script s? tÏm v‡ click v‡o Ù 'B?n dang nghi gÏ?'"):
            return False
        
        # Th? phÌm t?t 'c'
        try:
            from selenium.webdriver.common.action_chains import ActionChains
            actions = ActionChains(self.driver)
            actions.send_keys('c').perform()
            print("   ? –„ d˘ng phÌm t?t 'c'")
            time.sleep(2)
            return True
        except:
            pass
        
        # TÏm b?ng selector
        selectors = [
            "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'T?o b‡i vi?t')]",
            "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'Create a post')]",
            "//div[contains(text(), 'B?n dang nghi gÏ')]",
        ]
        
        for selector in selectors:
            try:
                elem = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if elem.is_displayed():
                    self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", elem)
                    print(f"   ? –„ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i")
                    time.sleep(2)
                    return True
            except:
                continue
        
        print("   ? KhÙng tÏm th?y Ù dang b‡i")
        return False
    
    def enter_content(self, content):
        """Nh?p n?i dung - t?ng bu?c"""
        
        print("\n?? N?I DUNG S? –ANG:")
        print("-" * 40)
        print(content)
        print("-" * 40)
        
        if not self.wait_for_user("NH?P N?I DUNG", "Script s? t? d?ng nh?p n?i dung trÍn v‡o khung so?n b‡i"):
            return False
        
        editor_selectors = [
            "//div[@role='textbox']",
            "//div[@contenteditable='true']",
        ]
        
        editor = None
        for selector in editor_selectors:
            try:
                editor = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if editor.is_displayed():
                    break
            except:
                continue
        
        if editor:
            try:
                editor.click()
            except:
                self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", editor)
            
            editor.send_keys(content)
            print("   ? –„ nh?p n?i dung")
            time.sleep(2)
            
            self.wait_for_user("KI?M TRA N?I DUNG", "H„y nhÏn trÏnh duy?t xem n?i dung d„ d˙ng chua?")
            return True
        else:
            print("   ? KhÙng tÏm th?y khung nh?p")
            return False
    
    def post(self):
        """–ang b‡i - t?ng bu?c"""
        
        if not self.wait_for_user("–ANG B¿I", "Script s? tÏm v‡ click n˙t –ang"):
            return False
        
        btn_selectors = [
            "//div[@aria-label='–ang']",
            "//div[@aria-label='Post']",
            "//div[contains(text(), '–ang')]",
        ]
        
        for selector in btn_selectors:
            try:
                btn = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, selector)
                if btn.is_displayed():
                    self.driver.execute_script("arguments[0].click();", btn)
                    print("   ? –„ click n˙t –ang")
                    time.sleep(3)
                    print("\n?? –ANG B¿I TH¿NH C‘NG!")
                    return True
            except:
                continue
        
        # Th? Ctrl+Enter
        try:
            editor = self.driver.find_element(By.XPATH, "//div[@role='textbox']")
            editor.send_keys(Keys.CONTROL, Keys.ENTER)
            print("   ? –„ d˘ng Ctrl+Enter")
            time.sleep(3)
            print("\n?? –ANG B¿I TH¿NH C‘NG!")
            return True
        except:
            print("   ? KhÙng th? dang b‡i")
            return False
    
    def close(self):
        if self.driver:
            self.driver.quit()
            print("?? –„ dÛng trÏnh duy?t")

def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("?? FACEBOOK POSTER - CH? –? T?NG BU?C")
    print("   B?n s? x·c nh?n t?ng thao t·c tru?c khi th?c hi?n")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    content = """Xin ch‡o b?n, hÙm nay ch˙ng ta s? c˘ng nhau di qua m?t h‡nh trÏnh nh? mang tÍn "BuÙng b?". 

CÛ nh?ng di?u trong cu?c s?ng khi?n ta n?ng lÚng, nhung dÙi khi, vi?c gi? ch?t l?i ch? l‡m ta thÍm m?t m?i. 

H„y th? hÌt m?t hoi th?t s‚uÖ v‡ th? ra th?t ch?mÖ d? c?m nh?n s? nh? nhım. 

B?n x?ng d·ng du?c bÏnh an, ngay trong kho?nh kh?c n‡y.

#BuongBo #BinhAn #TamLy

thÌ nghi?m 13 - Step by Step

Th‡nh cÙng!"""
    
    agent = StepByStepFacebookAgent()
    
    # T?ng bu?c cÛ x·c nh?n
    if not agent.login():
        print("? D?ng l?i do l?i dang nh?p")
        agent.close()
        return
    
    agent.handle_popups()
    
    if not agent.find_post_box():
        print("? KhÙng tÏm th?y Ù dang b‡i")
        agent.close()
        return
    
    if not agent.enter_content(content):
        print("? KhÙng th? nh?p n?i dung")
        agent.close()
        return
    
    agent.post()
    
    input("\n? HO¿N T?T! Nh?n Enter d? dÛng trÏnh duy?t...")
    agent.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import time
import pyautogui
from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from webdriver_manager.chrome import ChromeDriverManager
import json
import os

print("=" * 50)
print("?? FACEBOOK AUTO POSTER - PYAutoGUI")
print("=" * 50)

# N?i dung b‡i dang
content = '''Xin ch‡o b?n, hÙm nay ch˙ng ta s? c˘ng nhau di qua m?t h‡nh trÏnh nh? mang tÍn "BuÙng b?". 

CÛ nh?ng di?u trong cu?c s?ng khi?n ta n?ng lÚng, nhung dÙi khi, vi?c gi? ch?t l?i ch? l‡m ta thÍm m?t m?i. 

H„y th? hÌt m?t hoi th?t s‚uÖ v‡ th? ra th?t ch?mÖ d? c?m nh?n s? nh? nhım. 

B?n x?ng d·ng du?c bÏnh an, ngay trong kho?nh kh?c n‡y.

#BuongBo #BinhAn #TamLy

thÌ nghi?m 5 - T? d?ng ho‡n to‡n'''

# Copy n?i dung
import subprocess
subprocess.run("clip", input=content.encode("utf-8"), check=True)
print("? N?i dung d„ copy v‡o clipboard")

# M? trÏnh duy?t
print("?? –ang kh?i d?ng Chrome...")
options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
options.add_argument('--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled')
options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
options.add_argument('--disable-infobars')
service = Service(ChromeDriverManager().install())
driver = webdriver.Chrome(service=service, options=options)
driver.execute_script("Object.defineProperty(navigator, 'webdriver', {get: () => undefined})")

driver.get("https://www.facebook.com/")
time.sleep(3)

# Load cookie

if os.path.exists(cookie_file):
    with open(cookie_file, "r") as f:
        cookies = json.load(f)
    for cookie in cookies:
        try:
            driver.add_cookie(cookie)
        except:
            pass
    driver.refresh()
    time.sleep(5)
    print("? –„ dang nh?p!")

print("\n?? B?T –?U T? –?NG –ANG B¿I...")

# Ch? 3 gi‚y d? b?n chuy?n chu?t v‡o v? trÌ an to‡n
for i in range(3, 0, -1):
    print(f"   B?t d?u sau {i} gi‚y...")
    time.sleep(1)

# Bu?c 1: TÏm v‡ click v‡o Ù dang b‡i b?ng t?a d? (cÛ th? c?n di?u ch?nh)
print("?? Bu?c 1: Click v‡o Ù 'B?n dang nghi gÏ?'...")
# T?a d? m?c d?nh - B?n c?n ch?y l?y t?a d? th?c t?
# N?u khÙng click du?c, thay b?ng t?a d? ph˘ h?p v?i m‡n hÏnh c?a b?n
post_box_coords = (960, 250)  # (x, y) - C?N –I?U CH?NH
pyautogui.click(post_box_coords[0], post_box_coords[1])

--- FILE: fb_auto_undetected.py ---

import undetected_chromedriver as uc
import time
import json
import os

class FacebookAutoPoster:
    def __init__(self):
        self.driver = None
        self.cookie_file = "facebook_cookies.json"
    
    def start(self):
        """Kh?i d?ng trÏnh duy?t"""
        print("?? –ang kh?i d?ng trÏnh duy?t...")
        options = uc.ChromeOptions()
        options.add_argument('--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled')
        options.add_argument('--disable-dev-shm-usage')
        options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
        options.add_argument('--disable-infobars')
        options.add_argument('--lang=vi-VN')
        
        self.driver = uc.Chrome(options=options, version_main=None)
        return self.driver
    
    def login_with_cookie(self):
        """–ang nh?p b?ng cookie d„ luu"""
        if os.path.exists(self.cookie_file):
            print("?? –ang load cookies...")
            self.driver.get("https://www.facebook.com/")
            time.sleep(2)
            
            with open(self.cookie_file, "r") as f:
                cookies = json.load(f)
            
            for cookie in cookies:
                try:
                    self.driver.add_cookie(cookie)
                except:
                    pass
            
            self.driver.refresh()
            time.sleep(3)
            
            # Ki?m tra dang nh?p
            if "login" not in self.driver.current_url:
                print("? –„ dang nh?p b?ng cookie!")
                return True
        
        return self.login_manual()
    
    def login_manual(self):
        """–ang nh?p th? cÙng l?n d?u"""
        print("?? Vui lÚng dang nh?p TH? C‘NG...")
        print("?? Sau khi dang nh?p xong, nh?n Enter")
        
        self.driver.get("https://www.facebook.com/")
        input()
        
        # Luu cookie
        cookies = self.driver.get_cookies()
        with open(self.cookie_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(cookies, f)
        print("? –„ luu cookies!")
        return True
    
    def post(self, message):
        """–ang b‡i lÍn Facebook"""
        print(f"\n?? –ang dang b‡i: {message[:50]}...")
        
        # TÏm Ù t?o b‡i vi?t
        try:
            # C·ch 1: TÏm b?ng text
            post_box = self.driver.find_element("xpath", "//div[contains(@aria-label, 'T?o b‡i vi?t') or contains(@aria-label, 'Create a post')]")
            post_box.click()
            time.sleep(2)
            
            # TÏm khung nh?p
            editor = self.driver.find_element("xpath", "//div[@role='textbox' and @aria-label]")
            editor.click()
            editor.send_keys(message)
            time.sleep(2)
            
            # TÏm n˙t dang
            post_btn = self.driver.find_element("xpath", "//div[@aria-label='–ang' or @aria-label='Post']")
            post_btn.click()
            time.sleep(3)
            
            print("? –ang b‡i th‡nh cÙng!")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"? L?i: {e}")
            print("?? H„y dang b‡i TH? C‘NG trong trÏnh duy?t")
            input("?? Sau khi dang xong, nh?n Enter...")
            return False
    
    def close(self):
        if self.driver:
            self.driver.quit()

def main():
    print("=" * 50)
    print("?? FACEBOOK AUTO POSTER - UNDETECTED MODE")
    print("=" * 50)
    
    bot = FacebookAutoPoster()
    driver = bot.start()
    
    if bot.login_with_cookie():
        print("\n? S?n s‡ng dang b‡i!")
        
        # Nh?p n?i dung
        print("\n?? Nh?p n?i dung (Enter 2 l?n d? k?t th˙c):")
        lines = []
        while True:
            line = input()
            if line == "":
                break
            lines.append(line)
        
        message = "\n".join(lines)
        if message:
            bot.post(message)
        else:
            print("?? KhÙng cÛ n?i dung, b? qua")
    
    input("\nNh?n Enter d? dÛng...")
    bot.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

--- FILE: fb_auto_v2.py ---

from selenium import webdriver
from selenium.webdriver.chrome.service import Service
from webdriver_manager.chrome import ChromeDriverManager
from selenium.webdriver.common.by import By
from selenium.webdriver.common.keys import Keys
import time
import json
import os

print("=" * 50)
print("?? FACEBOOK AUTO POSTER - V2")
print("=" * 50)

# C?u hÏnh Chrome
options = webdriver.ChromeOptions()
options.add_argument('--disable-blink-features=AutomationControlled')
options.add_argument('--no-sandbox')
options.add_argument('--disable-infobars')
options.add_argument('--lang=vi-VN')
options.add_experimental_option('excludeSwitches', ['enable-automation'])
options.add_experimental_option('useAutomationExtension', False)

# T? d?ng t?i ChromeDriver
service = Service(ChromeDriverManager().install())

print("?? –ang kh?i d?ng Chrome...")

                elem.click()

                post_found = True
                break
        except:
            continue

        # C¡CH 3: TÏm t?t c? div button v‡ ki?m tra text

                editor.click()
                editor.send_keys(message)

                editor_found = True

            continue

        driver.execute_script(f"document.querySelector('[role=\"textbox\"]').innerText = '{message[:100]}'")

--- FILE: fb_scheduler.py ---

import schedule
import time
import subprocess
import datetime

def post_to_facebook():
    print(f"\n[{datetime.datetime.now()}] B?t d?u dang b‡i...")
    # G?i script dang b‡i
    subprocess.run(["python", "fb_auto_click.py"])
    print(f"[{datetime.datetime.now()}] –„ dang b‡i xong!")

# LÍn l?ch dang b‡i
# VÌ d?: dang b‡i l˙c 8:00, 12:00, 18:00 h‡ng ng‡y
schedule.every().day.at("08:00").do(post_to_facebook)
schedule.every().day.at("12:00").do(post_to_facebook)
schedule.every().day.at("18:00").do(post_to_facebook)

print("?? SCHEDULER FACEBOOK POSTER")
print("L?ch dang b‡i: 8:00, 12:00, 18:00 h‡ng ng‡y")
print("Nh?n Ctrl+C d? d?ng")

while True:
    schedule.run_pending()
    time.sleep(60)

--- FILE: fetch_accesstrade.py ---

import os
import requests
import psycopg2
import json
from datetime import datetime
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

ACCESS_KEY = os.getenv("ACCESS_TRADE_ACCESS_KEY")
if not ACCESS_KEY:
    raise ValueError("Ch∆∞a c√≥ ACCESS_TRADE_ACCESS_KEY trong .env")

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "sen_v3",
    "user": "postgres",
    "password": "0326014497",
    "host": "localhost",
    "port": 5432
}

def init_db():
    conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    cur.execute("""
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS campaigns (
            id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            campaign_id VARCHAR(50) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
            name TEXT,
            min_commission FLOAT,
            max_commission FLOAT,
            commission_type VARCHAR(20),
            category_id VARCHAR(20),
            category_name TEXT,
            logo TEXT,
            merchant TEXT,
            url TEXT,
            cookie_expire INT,
            status VARCHAR(10),
            raw_data JSONB,
            fetched_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
        )
    """)
    conn.commit()
    cur.close()
    conn.close()
    print("‚úÖ B·∫£ng campaigns ƒë√£ s·∫µn s√†ng")

def fetch_campaigns(page=1, page_size=50):
    url = "https://api.accesstrade.vn/v1/cashback/campaigns"
    headers = {
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
        "Authorization": f"Token {ACCESS_KEY}"
    }
    params = {"page": page, "page_size": page_size}
    resp = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=params)
    resp.raise_for_status()
    data = resp.json()
    if data.get("status") != "success":
        raise Exception(f"API error: {data.get('message')}")
    return data["data"]  # ch·ª©a campaigns v√† meta

def save_campaigns(campaigns):
    if not campaigns:
        return
    conn = psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    cur = conn.cursor()
    for camp in campaigns:
        campaign_id = str(camp.get("campaign_id"))
        name = camp.get("name", "")
        min_commission = float(camp.get("min_commission", 0))
        max_commission = float(camp.get("max_commission", 0))
        commission_type = camp.get("commission_type", "")
        category_id = camp.get("category_id", "")
        category_name = camp.get("category_name", "")
        logo = camp.get("logo", "")
        merchant = camp.get("merchant", "")
        url = camp.get("url", "")
        cookie_expire = camp.get("cookie_expire", 0)
        status = camp.get("status", "")

        cur.execute("""
            INSERT INTO campaigns (
                campaign_id, name, min_commission, max_commission,
                commission_type, category_id, category_name,
                logo, merchant, url, cookie_expire, status,
                raw_data, fetched_at
            ) VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, NOW())
            ON CONFLICT (campaign_id) DO UPDATE SET
                name = EXCLUDED.name,
                min_commission = EXCLUDED.min_commission,
                max_commission = EXCLUDED.max_commission,
                commission_type = EXCLUDED.commission_type,
                category_id = EXCLUDED.category_id,
                category_name = EXCLUDED.category_name,
                logo = EXCLUDED.logo,
                merchant = EXCLUDED.merchant,
                url = EXCLUDED.url,
                cookie_expire = EXCLUDED.cookie_expire,
                status = EXCLUDED.status,
                raw_data = EXCLUDED.raw_data,
                fetched_at = NOW()
        """, (
            campaign_id, name, min_commission, max_commission,
            commission_type, category_id, category_name,
            logo, merchant, url, cookie_expire, status,
            json.dumps(camp)
        ))
    conn.commit()
    cur.close()
    conn.close()
    print(f"‚úÖ ƒê√£ l∆∞u {len(campaigns)} campaign v√†o DB")

def fetch_all_campaigns():
    all_campaigns = []
    page = 1
    page_size = 50
    while True:
        print(f"üì° ƒêang l·∫•y trang {page}...")
        data = fetch_campaigns(page, page_size)
        campaigns = data.get("campaigns", [])
        if not campaigns:
            break
        all_campaigns.extend(campaigns)
        meta = data.get("meta", {})
        total = meta.get("total", 0)
        print(f"   L·∫•y {len(campaigns)} campaign, t·ªïng hi·ªán t·∫°i: {len(all_campaigns)}/{total}")
        if len(all_campaigns) >= total:
            break
        page += 1
    return all_campaigns

def fetch_and_store():
    init_db()
    campaigns = fetch_all_campaigns()
    if campaigns:
        save_campaigns(campaigns)
        print(f"üéâ T·ªïng c·ªông {len(campaigns)} campaign ƒë√£ ƒë∆∞·ª£c c·∫≠p nh·∫≠t.")
    else:
        print("‚ö†Ô∏è Kh√¥ng c√≥ campaign n√†o.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    fetch_and_store()

--- FILE: find_active_products.py ---

import asyncio
import aiohttp
import re
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

async def find_active_products():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("?? TÏm ki?m s?n ph?m dang b·n trÍn Lazada")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # C·c t? khÛa tÏm ki?m ph? bi?n
    keywords = ["di?n tho?i samsung", "laptop dell", "tai nghe bluetooth", "·o thun nam"]
    
    headers = {
        "User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36"
    }
    
    async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
        for keyword in keywords:
            search_url = f"https://www.lazada.vn/catalog/?q={keyword.replace(' ', '+')}"
            
            try:
                async with session.get(search_url, headers=headers) as resp:
                    if resp.status == 200:
                        html = await resp.text()
                        
                        # TÏm link s?n ph?m
                        pattern = r'https://www\.lazada\.vn/products/[^"?\s]+'
                        links = re.findall(pattern, html)
                        
                        # L?c link unique
                        unique_links = list(set(links))[:3]
                        
                        for link in unique_links:
                            print(f"\n?? {keyword}:")
                            print(f"   Link: {link}")
                            
                            # Th? l?y thÙng tin chi ti?t
                            async with session.get(link, headers=headers) as product_resp:
                                if product_resp.status == 200:
                                    product_html = await product_resp.text()
                                    
                                    # L?y tÍn s?n ph?m
                                    title_match = re.search(r'<title>(.*?)</title>', product_html)
                                    if title_match:
                                        title = title_match.group(1).replace('| Lazada.vn', '').strip()
                                        print(f"   TÍn: {title[:80]}")
                                    
                                    # L?y gi·
                                    price_match = re.search(r'<span[^>]*class="pdp-price"[^>]*>.*?(\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?)', product_html)
                                    if price_match:
                                        print(f"   Gi·: {price_match.group(1)} VND")
                            
                            await asyncio.sleep(1)  # Tr·nh rate limit
                    
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"? L?i tÏm ki?m {keyword}: {e}")
            
            await asyncio.sleep(2)
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(find_active_products())

--- FILE: find_active_products_v2.py ---

"""
Find active products on Lazada using Playwright
"""
import asyncio
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright

async def find_active_products():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("?? TÏm ki?m s?n ph?m dang b·n trÍn Lazada")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    products = []
    
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        page = await browser.new_page()
        
        # C·c t? khÛa tÏm ki?m
        keywords = ["di?n tho?i", "laptop", "tai nghe", "·o so mi"]
        
        for keyword in keywords:
            print(f"\n?? TÏm ki?m: {keyword}")
            
            search_url = f"https://www.lazada.vn/catalog/?q={keyword.replace(' ', '+')}"
            
            try:
                await page.goto(search_url, timeout=30000, wait_until="networkidle")
                await page.wait_for_timeout(3000)
                
                # L?y c·c link s?n ph?m
                product_links = await page.evaluate('''
                    () => {
                        const links = [];
                        const items = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/products/"]');
                        items.forEach(item => {
                            let href = item.getAttribute('href');
                            if (href && !href.includes('catalog')) {
                                links.push(href.startsWith('/') ? 'https://www.lazada.vn' + href : href);
                            }
                        });
                        return [...new Set(links)].slice(0, 3);
                    }
                ''')
                
                for link in product_links:
                    print(f"\n   ?? URL: {link}")
                    
                    # L?y chi ti?t s?n ph?m
                    try:
                        await page.goto(link, timeout=30000, wait_until="networkidle")
                        
                        # L?y tÍn
                        name = await page.evaluate('''
                            () => {
                                const selectors = ['h1', '[data-qa="product-name"]', '.pdp-product-title'];
                                for (let sel of selectors) {
                                    const el = document.querySelector(sel);
                                    if (el && el.innerText) return el.innerText.trim();
                                }
                                return null;
                            }
                        ''')
                        
                        # L?y gi·
                        price = await page.evaluate('''
                            () => {
                                const selectors = ['[data-qa="price"]', '.pdp-price', '.price'];
                                for (let sel of selectors) {
                                    const el = document.querySelector(sel);
                                    if (el && el.innerText) {
                                        const text = el.innerText;
                                        const match = text.match(/[\\d,.]+/);
                                        if (match) return match[0];
                                    }
                                }
                                return null;
                            }
                        ''')
                        
                        if name:
                            print(f"      ? TÍn: {name[:80]}")
                            print(f"      ?? Gi·: {price} VND" if price else "      ?? Gi·: N/A")
                            
                            # Luu s?n ph?m
                            products.append({
                                'name': name,
                                'url': link,
                                'price': price,
                                'keyword': keyword
                            })
                        else:
                            print(f"      ?? KhÙng th? l?y thÙng tin")
                            
                    except Exception as e:
                        print(f"      ? L?i: {e}")
                    
                    await asyncio.sleep(1)
                    
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"   ? L?i tÏm ki?m: {e}")
            
            await asyncio.sleep(2)
        
        await browser.close()
    
    # Hi?n th? k?t qu?
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print(f"?? K?T QU?: TÏm th?y {len(products)} s?n ph?m")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    for i, p in enumerate(products, 1):
        print(f"\n{i}. {p['name'][:100]}")
        print(f"   URL: {p['url']}")
        print(f"   Gi·: {p['price'] if p['price'] else 'N/A'} VND")
    
    # Luu v‡o file
    import json
    with open('active_products.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(products, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    print(f"\n? –„ luu {len(products)} s?n ph?m v‡o active_products.json")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    return products

async def main():
    try:
        products = await find_active_products()
        if not products:
            print("\n?? KhÙng tÏm th?y s?n ph?m n‡o.")
            print("?? G?i ˝: Website Lazada cÛ th? d„ thay d?i c?u tr˙c.")
            print("   H„y th? truy c?p th? cÙng: https://www.lazada.vn")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n? L?i: {e}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

--- FILE: find_lazada_skus.py ---

import asyncio
from playwright.async_api import async_playwright

async def find_products():
    print("?? Searching for products on Lazada...")
    
    async with async_playwright() as p:
        browser = await p.chromium.launch(headless=True)
        page = await browser.new_page()
        
        # Search for popular products
        search_terms = ["di?n tho?i", "laptop", "tai nghe", "smartphone"]
        
        all_skus = []
        
        for term in search_terms:
            print(f"\n?? Searching: {term}")
            search_url = f"https://www.lazada.vn/catalog/?q={term}"
            
            try:
                await page.goto(search_url, timeout=30000, wait_until="domcontentloaded")
                await page.wait_for_timeout(3000)
                
                # Get product links
                product_links = await page.evaluate('''
                    () => {
                        const links = [];
                        const items = document.querySelectorAll('a[href*="/products/"]');
                        items.forEach(item => {
                            let href = item.getAttribute('href');
                            if (href && !href.includes('catalog')) {
                                links.push(href.startsWith('/') ? 'https://www.lazada.vn' + href : href);
                            }
                        });
                        return [...new Set(links)].slice(0, 3);
                    }
                ''')
                
                for link in product_links:
                    # Extract SKU
                    import re
                    match = re.search(r'/products/([^/?]+)', link)
                    if match:
                        sku = match.group(1)
                        all_skus.append(sku)
                        print(f"   ? Found SKU: {sku}")
                        
            except Exception as e:
                print(f"   ?? Error: {e}")
        
        await browser.close()
        
        print(f"\n?? Total SKUs found: {len(all_skus)}")
        
        # Test each SKU
        print("\n?? Testing SKUs...")
        for sku in all_skus[:5]:  # Test first 5
            test_url = f"https://lazada.vn/products/{sku}"
            print(f"\n   Testing: {sku}")
            print(f"   URL: {test_url}")
            
    return all_skus

async def main():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("Lazada SKU Finder")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    skus = await find_products()
    
    print("\n" + "=" * 60)
    print("? Done! You can use these SKUs:")
    for sku in skus[:10]:
        print(f"   {sku}")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

            print(f"  ‚ö† {worker} co the thieu vong lap chinh")

    else:
        print(f"‚úó Missing: {worker}")

--- FILE: generate_full_report.py ---

"""
Full System Report - All Workers Data
"""
import sqlite3
import json
from datetime import datetime

def generate_full_report():
    conn = sqlite3.connect('sen_v3.db')
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    
    report = {
        "generated_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
        "workers": [],
        "tasks": {},
        "sales": {},
        "campaigns": {},
        "errors": []
    }
    
    # 1. Worker stats
    cursor.execute("SELECT worker_name, tasks_processed, tasks_succeeded, tasks_failed, status FROM worker_stats")
    for row in cursor.fetchall():
        report["workers"].append({
            "name": row[0],
            "processed": row[1],
            "succeeded": row[2],
            "failed": row[3],
            "status": row[4]
        })
    
    # 2. Task summary
    cursor.execute("SELECT task_type, status, COUNT(*) FROM tasks GROUP BY task_type, status")
    for row in cursor.fetchall():
        key = f"{row[0]}_{row[1]}"
        report["tasks"][key] = row[2]
    
    # 3. Sales summary
    cursor.execute("""
        SELECT 
            SUM(revenue) as total_revenue,
            SUM(commission) as total_commission,
            SUM(clicks) as total_clicks,
            SUM(orders) as total_orders
        FROM sales_tracking
    """)
    sales = cursor.fetchone()
    report["sales"] = {
        "total_revenue": sales[0] or 0,
        "total_commission": sales[1] or 0,
        "total_clicks": sales[2] or 0,
        "total_orders": sales[3] or 0
    }
    
    # 4. Campaign counts
    cursor.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM accesstrade_campaigns")
    report["campaigns"]["accesstrade"] = cursor.fetchone()[0]
    
    cursor.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM acfc_promotions WHERE status = 'active'")
    report["campaigns"]["acfc_active"] = cursor.fetchone()[0]
    
    cursor.execute("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM lazada_products")
    report["campaigns"]["lazada"] = cursor.fetchone()[0]
    
    # 5. Failed tasks
    cursor.execute("SELECT id, task_type, result FROM tasks WHERE status = 'failed' LIMIT 10")
    for row in cursor.fetchall():
        report["errors"].append({
            "task_id": row[0],
            "task_type": row[1],
            "result": row[2]
        })
    
    conn.close()
    
    # Save report
    with open('full_system_report.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(report, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    print("=" * 70)
    print("?? FULL SYSTEM REPORT GENERATED")
    print("=" * 70)
    print(f"\n?? WORKERS: {len(report['workers'])}")
    for w in report['workers']:
        print(f"   ? {w['name']}: {w['succeeded']}/{w['processed']} success ({w['status']})")
    
    print(f"\n?? SALES SUMMARY:")
    print(f"   ?? Revenue: {report['sales']['total_revenue']:,.0f} VND")
    print(f"   ?? Commission: {report['sales']['total_commission']:,.0f} VND")
    print(f"   ?? Clicks: {report['sales']['total_clicks']:,}")
    print(f"   ?? Orders: {report['sales']['total_orders']:,}")
    
    print(f"\n?? SUCCESS RATE:")
    total_tasks = sum(report['tasks'].values())
    completed = sum(v for k, v in report['tasks'].items() if 'completed' in k)
    print(f"   ? {completed}/{total_tasks} tasks completed ({completed/total_tasks*100:.1f}%)" if total_tasks > 0 else "   ? No tasks yet")
    
    print(f"\n?? Report saved: full_system_report.json")
    print("=" * 70)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generate_full_report()

--- FILE: generate_posts.py ---

"""
Generate bulk post content for social media
"""
import json
import sqlite3
from datetime import datetime

def generate_all_posts():
    """T?o n?i dung cho t?t c? campaigns"""
    
    conn = sqlite3.connect('sen_v3.db')
    cursor = conn.cursor()
    
    # L?y top campaigns
    cursor.execute("""
        SELECT id, name, category 
        FROM accesstrade_campaigns 
        WHERE category IN ('FINANCIAL SERVICES', '60', '35', 'E-COMMERCE')
        ORDER BY id
        LIMIT 30
    """)
    
    campaigns = cursor.fetchall()
    conn.close()
    
    publisher_id = "6983938396644077046"
    all_posts = []
    
    for campaign in campaigns:
        campaign_id = campaign[0]
        name = campaign[1]
        category = campaign[2]
        
        link = f"https://go.isclix.com/deep_link/v5/{publisher_id}/{campaign_id}?sub4=social_media"
        
        # Ch?n template theo category
        if 'FINANCIAL' in str(category) or '60' in str(category) or '35' in str(category):
            templates = [
                f"?? {name} - VAY TÕN CH?P L N –?N 500 TRI?U\n\n? Th? t?c don gi?n, gi?i ng‚n nhanh\n? L„i su?t uu d„i\n\n?? –ang k˝ ngay: {link}\n\n#VayVon #TaiChinh",
                f"?? {name}\n\n? SiÍu uu d„i t‡i chÌnh\n? Nh?n ngay h?n m?c cao\n? L„i su?t c?nh tranh\n\n?? –ang k˝: {link}",
                f"?? M? TH? TÕN D?NG {name}\n\n? 100% online, khÙng c?n ch?ng minh thu nh?p\n? Nh?n th? sau 3 ng‡y\n? Ho‡n ti?n d?n 5%\n\n?? M? th? ngay: {link}"
            ]
        else:
            templates = [
                f"??? {name} - MUA S?M GI¡ S?C\n\n? Gi?m gi· d?n 50%\n? Free ship don t? 200K\n? Nh?n voucher h?p d?n\n\n?? Mua ngay: {link}",
                f"?? FLASH SALE - {name}\n\n? Gi?m s?c d?n 70%\n? S? lu?ng cÛ h?n\n\n?? San deal ngay: {link}"
            ]
        
        import random
        content = random.choice(templates)
        
        all_posts.append({
            'id': campaign_id,
            'name': name,
            'category': category,
            'content': content,
            'link': link,
            'generated_at': datetime.now().isoformat()
        })
    
    # Luu t?t c? b‡i dang
    with open('all_posts.json', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(all_posts, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    # T?o file d? copy
    with open('posts_to_copy.txt', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write("=" * 80 + "\n")
        f.write("?? N?I DUNG B¿I –ANG M?NG X√ H?I\n")
        f.write("=" * 80 + "\n\n")
        
        for i, post in enumerate(all_posts, 1):
            f.write(f"\n?? B¿I –ANG #{i}\n")
            f.write("-" * 40 + "\n")
            f.write(f"{post['content']}\n")
            f.write("-" * 40 + "\n\n")
    
    print("=" * 70)
    print(f"? –„ t?o {len(all_posts)} b‡i dang")
    print("?? File d„ t?o:")
    print("   - all_posts.json (d? li?u JSON)")
    print("   - posts_to_copy.txt (n?i dung d? copy)")
    print("=" * 70)
    
    # Hi?n th? m?u
    print("\n?? M?U B¿I –ANG:")
    print("-" * 70)
    for i, post in enumerate(all_posts[:3], 1):
        print(f"\nB‡i {i}: {post['name'][:50]}")
        print(f"   {post['content'][:100]}...")
        print(f"   Link: {post['link'][:80]}...")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generate_all_posts()

--- FILE: generate_report.py ---

"""
Revenue Report Generator for AccessTrade
"""
import json
from datetime import datetime

def generate_report():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("?? ACCESSTRADE REVENUE REPORT")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    # –?c tracking data
    try:
        with open('order_tracking.json', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            data = json.load(f)
    except:
        print("? No tracking data found. Run create_tracking.py first")
        return
    
    products = data['products']
    
    # TÌnh t?ng
    total_clicks = sum(p['clicks'] for p in products)
    total_orders = sum(p['orders'] for p in products)
    total_revenue = sum(p['revenue'] for p in products)
    total_commission = sum(p['commission'] for p in products)
    
    print(f"\n?? SUMMARY STATISTICS:")
    print(f"   Total Products: {len(products)}")
    print(f"   Total Clicks: {total_clicks}")
    print(f"   Total Orders: {total_orders}")
    print(f"   Total Revenue: {total_revenue:,.0f} VND")
    print(f"   Total Commission: {total_commission:,.0f} VND")
    
    print(f"\n?? PRODUCT PERFORMANCE:")
    for idx, p in enumerate(products, 1):
        print(f"\n   {idx}. {p['name'][:50]}")
        print(f"      Clicks: {p['clicks']}")
        print(f"      Orders: {p['orders']}")
        print(f"      Revenue: {p['revenue']:,.0f} VND")
        print(f"      Commission: {p['commission']:,.0f} VND")
        if p['clicks'] > 0:
            conversion_rate = (p['orders'] / p['clicks']) * 100
            print(f"      Conversion Rate: {conversion_rate:.1f}%")
    
    # T?o file b·o c·o
    report_file = f'report_{datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")}.json'
    with open(report_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)
    
    print(f"\n? Report saved to {report_file}")
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    generate_report()

--- FILE: get_accesstrade_campaigns.py ---

"""
Get AccessTrade Campaigns - Real Data
"""
import asyncio
import sys
from pathlib import Path

sys.path.insert(0, str(Path(__file__).parent))

from src.accesstrade_client import get_accesstrade_client

async def get_campaigns():
    print("=" * 60)
    print("?? AccessTrade Campaigns - REAL DATA")
    print("=" * 60)
    
    client = await get_accesstrade_client()
    result = await client.get_campaigns(limit=10)
    
    if result.get('success'):
        campaigns = result.get('data', [])
        print(f"\n? Found {len(campaigns)} campaigns:\n")
        
        for idx, camp in enumerate(campaigns[:10], 1):
            name = camp.get('name', 'N/A')
            commission = camp.get('commission', 'N/A')
            print(f"{idx}. {name[:60]}")
            print(f"   Commission: {commission}%")
            print()
    else:
        print(f"? Error: {result.get('error')}")
    
    await client.close()
    print("=" * 60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(get_campaigns())

import asyncio
import requests
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

access_key = os.getenv("ACCESSTRADE_ACCESS_KEY")
headers = {"Authorization": f"Token {access_key}"}

print("=" * 60)
print("?? AccessTrade Campaigns - REAL DATA")
print("=" * 60)

response = requests.get(
    "https://api.accesstrade.vn/v1/campaigns",
    headers=headers,
    params={"limit": 20}
)

if response.status_code == 200:
    data = response.json()
    campaigns = data.get('data', [])
    print(f"\n? Found {len(campaigns)} campaigns:\n")
    
    for idx, camp in enumerate(campaigns[:10], 1):
        name = camp.get('name', 'N/A')
        commission = camp.get('commission', 'N/A')
        print(f"{idx}. {name[:70]}")
        print(f"   Commission: {commission}%")
        print()
else:
    print(f"? Error: {response.status_code}")

print("=" * 60)

--- FILE: get_coords.py ---

import pyautogui
import time

print("=" * 50)
print("?? TOOL L?Y T?A –? CHU?T")
print("=" * 50)
print("\nHu?ng d?n:")
print("1. Di chuy?n chu?t d?n v? trÌ c?n l?y t?a d?")
print("2. Nh?n 'c' d? ghi nh?n t?a d?")
print("3. Nh?n 'q' d? tho·t\n")

positions = []

while True:
    x, y = pyautogui.position()
    print(f"   T?a d? hi?n t?i: ({x}, {y})", end="\r")
    
    # Ki?m tra phÌm b?m
    try:
        import msvcrt
        if msvcrt.kbhit():
            key = msvcrt.getch().decode('utf-8').lower()
            if key == 'c':
                positions.append((x, y))
                print(f"\n? –„ luu t?a d?: ({x}, {y})")
            elif key == 'q':
                print("\n\n?? DANH S¡CH T?A –? –√ LUU:")
                for i, pos in enumerate(positions):
                    print(f"   {i+1}. ({pos[0]}, {pos[1]})")
                break
    except:
        pass
    
    time.sleep(0.1)

--- FILE: get_fresh_token.py ---

import requests
import webbrowser
from urllib.parse import urlencode
from dotenv import set_key

CLIENT_KEY = "awa6cdjba8pizprl"
CLIENT_SECRET = "hGLKRm0zJyQx9fMObmIP22MTk5JiMH86"
REDIRECT_URI = "https://your-domain.com/callback"

# T?o URL ?y quy?n
params = {
    "client_key": CLIENT_KEY,
    "response_type": "code",
    "scope": "user.info.basic,video.upload,video.publish",
    "redirect_uri": REDIRECT_URI,
}
auth_url = "https://www.tiktok.com/v2/auth/authorize/?" + urlencode(params)

print("=" * 60)
print("?? L?Y M√ CODE TIKTOK")
print("=" * 60)
print("\n?? Truy c?p URL sau:")
print(auth_url)
print("\n?? Sau khi ?y quy?n, copy m„ 'code' t? URL")
print("=" * 60)

webbrowser.open(auth_url)

# Nh?p m„ code
auth_code = input("\n?? D·n m„ code v‡o d‚y: ").strip()

if not auth_code:
    print("? Chua nh?p m„ code!")
    exit()

# –?i code l?y token
url = "https://open.tiktokapis.com/v2/oauth/token/"
data = {
    "client_key": CLIENT_KEY,
    "client_secret": CLIENT_SECRET,
    "code": auth_code,
    "grant_type": "authorization_code",
    "redirect_uri": REDIRECT_URI,
}
headers = {"Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"}

response = requests.post(url, data=data, headers=headers)
result = response.json()

print("\n" + "=" * 60)
if "access_token" in result:
    print("? TH¿NH C‘NG!")
    print(f"   Access Token: {result['access_token'][:50]}...")
    print(f"   Open ID: {result.get('open_id')}")
    
    # Luu v‡o .env
    set_key(".env", "TIKTOK_ACCESS_TOKEN", result['access_token'])
    set_key(".env", "TIKTOK_OPEN_ID", result.get('open_id', ''))
    print("\n? –„ luu token m?i v‡o .env")
else:
    print(f"? L?I: {result.get('error')}")
    print(f"   {result.get('error_description', '')}")
print("=" * 60)

--- FILE: get_page_id.py ---

import requests
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

token = os.getenv('FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN')

if not token or 'your_' in token:
    print("? Token chua du?c c?u hÏnh d˙ng trong .env")
    exit(1)

print("=" * 50)
print("?? DANH S¡CH TRANG C?A B?N")
print("=" * 50)

url = f'https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/me/accounts?access_token={token}'

try:
    response = requests.get(url)
    data = response.json()
    
    if 'data' in data:
        for page in data['data']:
            print(f"\n?? TÍn trang: {page.get('name')}")
            print(f"?? Page ID: {page.get('id')}")
            print(f"?? Token: {page.get('access_token')[:50]}...")
            print("-" * 40)
        
        if data['data']:
            print(f"\n? TÏm th?y {len(data['data'])} trang")
            print("\n?? COPY Page ID v‡ thÍm v‡o .env:")
            print('   FACEBOOK_PAGE_ID=' + data['data'][0]['id'])
        else:
            print("? KhÙng tÏm th?y trang n‡o. H„y t?o Fanpage tru?c.")
    else:

except Exception as e:
    print(f"? L?i k?t n?i: {e}")

--- FILE: grader.py ---

import json
import re
from typing import Dict, List

class Grader:
    def __init__(self, expectations: List[Dict]):
        """
        expectations = [
            {"text": "B√†i vi·∫øt c√≥ ch·ª©a link affiliate", "regex": r"https?://.*affiliate.*"},
            {"text": "ƒê·ªô d√†i > 50 k√Ω t·ª±", "min_length": 50},
            {"text": "C√≥ t·ª´ kh√≥a 'hoa h·ªìng'", "regex": r"hoa h·ªìng"},
            {"text": "C√≥ c·∫£m x√∫c t√≠ch c·ª±c", "positive_words": ["si√™u", "hot", "xu h∆∞·ªõng", "ki·∫øm ti·ªÅn"]}
        ]
        """
        self.expectations = expectations

    def grade(self, article: str) -> Dict:
        results = []
        for exp in self.expectations:
            passed = False
            evidence = ""
            if "regex" in exp:
                if re.search(exp["regex"], article, re.IGNORECASE):
                    passed = True
                    evidence = f"T√¨m th·∫•y pattern: {exp['regex']}"
                else:
                    evidence = "Kh√¥ng t√¨m th·∫•y pattern"
            elif "min_length" in exp:
                if len(article) >= exp["min_length"]:
                    passed = True
                    evidence = f"ƒê·ªô d√†i {len(article)} >= {exp['min_length']}"
                else:
                    evidence = f"ƒê·ªô d√†i {len(article)} < {exp['min_length']}"
            elif "positive_words" in exp:
                words = exp["positive_words"]
                found = [w for w in words if w in article.lower()]
                if found:
                    passed = True
                    evidence = f"C√°c t·ª´ t√≠ch c·ª±c: {', '.join(found)}"
                else:
                    evidence = "Kh√¥ng c√≥ t·ª´ t√≠ch c·ª±c n√†o"
            else:
                # fallback
                passed = False
                evidence = "Kh√¥ng r√µ expectation"
            results.append({
                "text": exp["text"],
                "passed": passed,
                "evidence": evidence
            })
        total = len(results)
        passed_count = sum(1 for r in results if r["passed"])
        return {
            "expectations": results,
            "summary": {
                "passed": passed_count,
                "failed": total - passed_count,
                "total": total,
                "pass_rate": passed_count / total if total > 0 else 0
            }
        }

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Test
    sample_article = "üåü Si√™u sale! Chi·∫øn d·ªãch th·ªùi trang m√πa h√® hoa h·ªìng l√™n t·ªõi 12.5%. Mua ngay t·∫°i https://shopee.com/affiliate/123"
    expectations = [
        {"text": "C√≥ link affiliate", "regex": r"https?://.*affiliate"},
        {"text": "ƒê·ªô d√†i > 30", "min_length": 30},
        {"text": "C√≥ t·ª´ 'hoa h·ªìng'", "regex": r"hoa h·ªìng"},
        {"text": "C√≥ t·ª´ t√≠ch c·ª±c", "positive_words": ["si√™u", "hot"]}
    ]
    g = Grader(expectations)
    result = g.grade(sample_article)
    print(json.dumps(result, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))

import os
import requests
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()

def check_gemini():
    print("üîç Ki·ªÉm tra Gemini API...", end=" ")
    key = os.getenv("GEMINI_API_KEY")
    # Th·ª±c hi·ªán g·ªçi th·ª≠ m·ªôt endpoint ƒë∆°n gi·∫£n c·ªßa Google AI
    # (S·ª≠ d·ª•ng th∆∞ vi·ªán google-generativeai n·∫øu b·∫°n ƒë√£ c√†i)
    if not key or key.startswith("your_"):
        print("‚ùå L·ªói: Key ch∆∞a c·∫•u h√¨nh")
        return
    print("‚úÖ ƒê√£ c·∫•u h√¨nh key (C·∫ßn x√°c th·ª±c qua library)")

def check_facebook():
    print("üîç Ki·ªÉm tra Facebook Token...", end=" ")
    token = os.getenv("FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN")
    url = f"https://graph.facebook.com/v21.0/me?access_token={token}"
    try:
        response = requests.get(url)
        if response.status_code == 200:
            print("‚úÖ H·ª£p l·ªá!")
        else:
            print(f"‚ùå L·ªói: {response.json().get('error', {}).get('message')}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"‚ùå L·ªói k·∫øt n·ªëi: {e}")

    check_facebook()
